msg:A hotel whose quality far exceeds its price, this is a highly recommended local hotel in Yuyao.

Normally it costs about 400 per night for two breakfasts, but the result of staying here far exceeded expectations!

Let me start by boasting about the breakfast, which can even be said to be luxurious! Better than many big-name chains selling for thousands of dollars! The noodle stall has Ningbo specialty yellow croaker noodles, and there are no limited quantities. Other choices are also very rich, including Yuyao special sauce duck, big cakes, etc. The noodle stall is also very strong. Many items are freshly made by the aunt, and there are even unlimited shrimp dumplings. .

The Western food stall also offers bacon, chicken drumsticks, egg tarts, etc. Although the juice is a bit weak, it also provides fresh yogurt!

The room is big enough, a little bigger than the hotel's own promotional picture, and spacious enough.

The service is also good, the number of fruits delivered exceeds that of the Nanjing Ritz-Carlton, and sweet soup is also delivered in the evening.
